Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

$265.00/haul

$257.40/haul

Hello,

Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

$265.00/haul

Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

$265.00/haul

$88.34 disposal/ton

 

Bid #1: Waste Management

$227.08/haul

$43.05 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Bid #2: GFL

$257.40/haul

$71.50 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Quotes are valid for 30 days.  Rates are per compactor, and do not include any applicable taxes/fees.

Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

$265.00/haul

$88.34 disposal/ton

$227.08/haul

$43.05 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Bid #2: GFL

$257.40/haul

$71.50 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

 

Current: Republic Services

$265.00/haul

$88.34 disposal/ton

 

Bid #1: Waste Management

$227.08/haul

$43.05 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Bid #2: GFL

$257.40/haul

$71.50 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Quotes are valid for 30 days.  Rates are per compactor, and do not include any applicable taxes/fees.

 

I have attached the information again on how to access the Waste Portal for equipment quotes, if needed.

Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

 

Current: Republic Services

$265.00/haul

$88.34 disposal/ton

 

Bid #1: Waste Management

$227.08/haul

$43.05 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Bid #2: GFL

$257.40/haul

$71.50 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Quotes are valid for 30 days.  Rates are per compactor, and do not include any applicable taxes/fees.

 

I have attached the information again on how to access the Waste Portal for equipment quotes, if needed.

 

If you have any questions, please let me know.

Hello,

 

Apologies for the delayed response on this matter.  We were awaiting Republic’s response on any costs associated with removing their equipment, which was finally provided.

 

While our records show that the agreement is still active for Jones Grant, Republic Services is indicating that they now have it on a month-to-month status.  Therefore, if the property wishes to cancel, there would be no liquidated damages involved.

 

You are currently paying $883.35 per compactor for the rental to Republic.  To remove the existing compactor equipment, there would be a $1,540.00 charge, per unit, to uninstall the compactors.  Once requested, it typically takes 15-20 days to schedule the removal.

 

Greystar would handle procuring the replacement equipment through their preferred equipment vendors, CRA and Tower. 

 

You could either continue to utilize Republic to service the replacement equipment, or potentially switch to an alternate vendor.  Below are quotes from both WM and an alternate third party vendor for review.  Note, quotes are for service only; If the property were to lease that equipment, the lease cost would likely be able to be added to the consolidated invoice/ WM would be able to pay the lease cost on behalf of the property.

 

Current: Republic Services

$265.00/haul

$88.34 disposal/ton

 

Bid #1: Waste Management

$227.08/haul

$43.05 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Bid #2: GFL

$257.40/haul

$71.50 disposal/ton (3 ton minimum)

 

Quotes are valid for 30 days.  Rates are per compactor, and do not include any applicable taxes/fees.

 

I have attached the information again on how to access the Waste Portal for equipment quotes, if needed.

 

If you have any questions, please let me know.

 

Thank you,

 

Dawn M. Opolony

Program Manager I, Commercial Properties
